highways and Minor ports Department

Tamil Nadu Highways Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 66, Highways and Minor Ports (HF1), 8th July 2019, ÝQ 23, Mè£K,  
F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2050.]
No. II(2)/HWMP/773/2019.
In exercise of the powers conferred by Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 
34 of 2002), the Governor of Tamil Nadu, on the recommendation made by the State Highways Authority, 
hereby declares that the roads specified in the Annexure to be Highways and classifies them as State 
Highways, Major District Roads and Other District Roads as indicated therein.
